				var att=document.createAttribute("data-style-type");
				att.value="ls";
				var style = document.createElement("style");
					script = document.getElementsByTagName("script");
				style.setAttributeNode(att);
				style.type = "text/css";
				style.appendChild(document.createTextNode(css));
				script[0].parentNode.insertBefore(style, script[0]);
			}else{
				window.scrollTo(0,0);
			}
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   var ajax_url = "http://www.lifehack.org/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php";
  </script>
 </head>

       <div class="span6" id="article-content">
        <header class="visible-desktop">
         <h1 class="nolinks btitle-replacable">
          The Ultimate Wanderlist: 60 Cities To Visit Before You Die
         </h1>
         <span class="meta">
          <span class="info">
           <span class="category">
            <a href="/lifestyle/leisure" rel="category tag" title="View all posts in Leisure">
             Leisure
            </a>
            <a href="/lifestyle" rel="category tag" title="View all posts in Lifestyle">
             Lifestyle
            </a>
           </span>
           by
           <a href="/author/hiba-argane" rel="author" title="Posts by Hiba Argane">
            Hiba Argane
           </a>
           <span class="total-share-text">
            <span class="separator">
             |
            </span>
            8K Shares
           </span>
          </span>
          <span>
           <span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </header>
        <div class="google-text-ad">
        </div>
        <div class="div-gpt-ad-content-top adslot visible-desktop" data-dfp="Lifehack_Content_Top_640x180" id="div-gpt-ad-content-top-1" style="width:640px; height:180px;">
        </div>
        <div class="adslot hidden-desktop" data-dfp="Lifehack_Content_Mobile_320x100" id="div-gpt-ad-content-mobile-1" style="width:320px; height:100px; margin-bottom: 25px;">
        </div>
        <div class="post-content">
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          Its never too late to go on a holiday youll never forget. Or 60 holidays! Heres a list of 60 of the best cities to visit, according to tourists around the globe. It will give you a littleglimpse ofeach location with three suggested attractions or activities that are a must-see (or do!) while you are there. Read on and maybe youll be a little inspired to start planning the ultimate holiday.
         </p>
         <h2>
          1. Los Angeles, USA
         </h2>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter wp-image-200715 size-large" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 66.56%">
            <img alt="Hollywood_boulevard_from_kodak_theatre" bgcolor="#765f54" class="lazy-img aligncenter wp-image-200715 size-large" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Hollywood_boulevard_from_kodak_theatre-1024x682.jpg","width":1500,"height":1000}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Hollywood_boulevard_from_kodak_theatre-1024x682.jpg","width":1024,"height":682}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Hollywood_boulevard_from_kodak_theatre-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Hollywood_boulevard_from_kodak_theatre-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="Hollywood_boulevard_from_kodak_theatre" height="426" src="http://cdn-media-1.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/Hollywood_boulevard_from_kodak_theatre-1024x682.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          Sunny LA with all its energetic buzz of dreamers and go-getters, it can be superficial but also multicultural and complex. Visiting Hollywood, the birthplace of the iconic Mickey Mouse, and taking selfies on the Star Walk of Fame are just a snippet of the LA experience.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Visit
           <a href="http://www.lonelyplanet.com/usa/los-angeles/sights/museums-galleries/getty-center" target="_blank">
            Getty Center
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           <span style="line-height: 1.5em;">
            Visit
            <a href="http://www.lacma.org/" target="_blank">
             Lacma Museum
            </a>
           </span>
          </li>
          <li>
           <span style="line-height: 1.5em;">
            Shop vintage at
           </span>
           <a href="http://www.lonelyplanet.com/usa/los-angeles/shopping/fashion-accessories/raggedy-threads" style="line-height: 1.5em;" target="_blank">
            Raggedy Threads
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          2. Marrakech, Morocco
         </h2>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200716" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 66.41%">
            <img alt="Maroc_Marrakech_Jemaa-el-Fna_Luc_Viatour" bgcolor="#ac8c78" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200716" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Maroc_Marrakech_Jemaa-el-Fna_Luc_Viatour-1024x680.jpg","width":3008,"height":2000}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Maroc_Marrakech_Jemaa-el-Fna_Luc_Viatour-1024x680.jpg","width":1024,"height":680}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Maroc_Marrakech_Jemaa-el-Fna_Luc_Viatour-380x252.jpg","width":380,"height":252}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Maroc_Marrakech_Jemaa-el-Fna_Luc_Viatour-380x252.jpg","width":380,"height":252}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="Maroc_Marrakech_Jemaa-el-Fna_Luc_Viatour" height="425" src="http://cdn-media-1.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/Maroc_Marrakech_Jemaa-el-Fna_Luc_Viatour-1024x680.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          Pulsating with stunning mosques, fascinating crafts and luxury living, Marrakech is a very popular destination amongst travellers. Whether youd like to circle the Koutoubia mosque or enjoy a culinary high with a side of modern art, its all here from the exotic to the hypnotic.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Take a walk around
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.co.uk/Attraction_Review-g293734-d318047-Reviews-Jemaa_el_Fna-Marrakech_Marrakech_Tensift_El_Haouz_Region.html" target="_blank">
            Jemaa el Fna
           </a>
           and all its souks
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.co.uk/Attraction_Review-g293734-d477277-Reviews-Jardin_Majorelle-Marrakech_Marrakech_Tensift_El_Haouz_Region.html" target="_blank">
            Jardins Majorelle
           </a>
           at Rue Yves Saint Laurent
          </li>
          <li>
           <span style="line-height: 1.5em;">
            Bargain at the busy
           </span>
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.co.uk/Attraction_Review-g293734-d550588-Reviews-Rahba_Kedima_Square-Marrakech_Marrakech_Tensift_El_Haouz_Region.html" style="line-height: 1.5em;" target="_blank">
            Rahba Kedima Square
           </a>
           <span style="line-height: 1.5em;">
           </span>
          </li>

         <h2>
          3. New York City, USA
         </h2>
         <p style="text-align: justify;">
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200717" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 66.56%">
            <img alt="new_york_hop" bgcolor="#5d5e65" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200717" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/new_york_hop-1024x682.jpg","width":3840,"height":2560}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/new_york_hop-1024x682.jpg","width":1024,"height":682}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/new_york_hop-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/new_york_hop-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}'/>

         <p>
          If youre a first-timer, go ahead and be as touristy as possible. Visit the Statue of Liberty, Times Square, the Met, Central Park  But if youve got more time, be sure to delve into the neighborhoods because youll surely find quirky shops, delis and hole-in-the-wall bars. Its an incredibly rewarding experience to go behind the scenes here.

           stroll

           </a>

         <h2>
          4. Chiang Mai, Thailand
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200718" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 67.66%">
            <img alt="CNX Chiang Mai Waterfalls" bgcolor="#776b55" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200718" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/CNX-Chiang-Mai-Waterfalls-1024x694.jpg","width":1274,"height":864}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/CNX-Chiang-Mai-Waterfalls-1024x694.jpg","width":1024,"height":694}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/CNX-Chiang-Mai-Waterfalls-380x257.jpg","width":380,"height":257}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/CNX-Chiang-Mai-Waterfalls-380x257.jpg","width":380,"height":257}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="CNX Chiang Mai Waterfalls" height="433" src="http://cdn-media-1.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/CNX-Chiang-Mai-Waterfalls-1024x694.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          Chiang Mai is laid back, vibrant and reverential. Explore the famous Night Bazaar, the National Museum, and the Botanic Gardens to soak up as much of the culture and exquisite aromas of Thai orchids as possible. Spiritual vibes are also at an all-time high here with the citys center being home to over 30 temples.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Try khao soi (nothing says Im in Chiang Mai more than that!)
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.co.uk/Attraction_Review-g293917-d657510-Reviews-Doi_Suthep_Pui_National_Park-Chiang_Mai.html" target="_blank">
            Doi Suthep-Pui National Park
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Wait for a sunny day and go on a
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.co.uk/Attraction_Review-g1961657-d1961277-Reviews-Balloon_Adventure_Thailand-Doi_Saket.html" target="_blank">
            Balloon Adventure
           </a>
           for a whole different view of the city
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          5. Budapest, Hungary
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200719" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 62.5%">
            <img alt="c64c7908bff8748b5c81434bb4c48bdb123e330f" bgcolor="#31597d" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200719" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/c64c7908bff8748b5c81434bb4c48bdb123e330f-1024x640.jpg","width":1920,"height":1200}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/c64c7908bff8748b5c81434bb4c48bdb123e330f-1024x640.jpg","width":1024,"height":640}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/c64c7908bff8748b5c81434bb4c48bdb123e330f-380x237.jpg","width":380,"height":237}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/c64c7908bff8748b5c81434bb4c48bdb123e330f-380x237.jpg","width":380,"height":237}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="c64c7908bff8748b5c81434bb4c48bdb123e330f" height="400" src="http://cdn-media-1.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/c64c7908bff8748b5c81434bb4c48bdb123e330f-1024x640.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          Budapest is a gem of Baroque, neoclassical, eclectic and Secessionist buildings to satisfy the architectural cravings of its eager visitors. Not your thing? Well, Budapest has more to offer, from the poignant scars of war and history, to an abundance of thermal and mineral hot springs, so the options are numerous.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Take a
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.co.uk/Attraction_Review-g274887-d3155869-Reviews-Dinner_Cruise_on_Danube_Mahart_Passnave_Day_Boat_Tours-Budapest_Central_Hungary.html" target="_blank">
            Danube cruise
           </a>
           for a stunning panoramic view
          </li>
          <li>
           Take a dip at one of Budapests famous baths
          </li>
          <li>
           Walk across
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.co.uk/Attraction_Review-g274887-d276821-Reviews-Chain_Bridge_Szechenyi_lanchid-Budapest_Central_Hungary.html" target="_blank">
            Chain Bridge
           </a>
           and youll understand why its often called the Pearl of the Danube
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          6. Krakow, Poland
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200720" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 71.72%">
            <img alt="Krakow_rynek_01" bgcolor="#9a9288" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200720" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Krakow_rynek_01-1024x735.jpg","width":1825,"height":1310}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Krakow_rynek_01-1024x735.jpg","width":1024,"height":735}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Krakow_rynek_01-380x272.jpg","width":380,"height":272}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Krakow_rynek_01-380x272.jpg","width":380,"height":272}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="Krakow_rynek_01" height="459" src="http://cdn-media-1.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/Krakow_rynek_01-1024x735.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          Krakow is Polands second largest city covering both banks of the Wisla River. To many first-timers its easy to feel at home very quickly in its old-world ambiance and charm. Old Town and Kazimierzs streets are crammed with galleries, cafs, pubs and restaurants, all for your touristic enjoyment.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Visit
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.co.uk/Attraction_Review-g274772-d1534527-Reviews-Krakow_s_Historic_Centre-Krakow_Lesser_Poland_Province_Southern_Poland.html" target="_blank">
            Krakows Historic Centre
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Go shopping at the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.co.uk/Attraction_Review-g274772-d276740-Reviews-Main_Market_Square-Krakow_Lesser_Poland_Province_Southern_Poland.html" target="_blank">
            Main Market Square
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Take a walk down the chilling
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.co.uk/Attraction_Review-g274772-d6158750-Reviews-Lost_Souls_Alley-Krakow_Lesser_Poland_Province_Southern_Poland.html" target="_blank">
            Lost Souls Alley
           </a>
           interactive museum
          </li>
         </ul>

         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200721" style="max-width: 640px">

           </a>
           and relive some overwhelming history
          </li>
          <li>

         </h2>

          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200723" style="max-width: 640px">

         <h2>
          9. Florence, Italy
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200725" style="max-width: 640px">

            Cinema teatro Odeon
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           For the ultimate shopping experience,
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g187895-d3717792-Reviews-Janniderma-Florence_Tuscany.html" target="_blank">

           </a>
           is the place

         <h2>
          10. London, England
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200727" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 75.78%">
            <img alt="grossbritannien_london_eye" bgcolor="#6b5355" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200727" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/grossbritannien_london_eye-1024x776.jpg","width":1800,"height":1365}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/grossbritannien_london_eye-1024x776.jpg","width":1024,"height":776}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/grossbritannien_london_eye-380x288.jpg","width":380,"height":288}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/grossbritannien_london_eye-380x288.jpg","width":380,"height":288}'/>
           </span>

         <p>
          The ultimate cocktail of history, art, fashion and food in one place, thats London! Theres a little something for everyone from the Tate Modern and the Royal Opera House for the art fanatics, Oxford Street shops for the ones willing to splurge, and Abbey Road and the Sherlock Holmes Museum for the music and book lovers.

           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g186338-d1063660-Reviews-The_O2-London_England.html" target="_blank">
            O2
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           The king of specialty shops in London,
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g186338-d3923313-Reviews-Forbidden_Planet-London_England.html" target="_blank">

         <h2>
          11. Riga, Latvia
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200728" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 66.56%">
            <img alt="walking_in_riga_by_tori_tolkacheva-d71qdfq" bgcolor="#6e6f6e" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200728" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/walking_in_riga_by_tori_tolkacheva-d71qdfq-1024x682.jpg","width":1095,"height":730}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/walking_in_riga_by_tori_tolkacheva-d71qdfq-1024x682.jpg","width":1024,"height":682}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/walking_in_riga_by_tori_tolkacheva-d71qdfq-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/walking_in_riga_by_tori_tolkacheva-d71qdfq-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="walking_in_riga_by_tori_tolkacheva-d71qdfq" height="426" src="http://cdn-media-1.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/walking_in_riga_by_tori_tolkacheva-d71qdfq-1024x682.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          This city is the largest metropolisin the Baltics and its a compelling mix of Latvian traditions and influences from various other countries. Riga is funky and vibrant, trapping travelers long past their departure date. Riga manages to combine its steeples and turrets with an irresistible nightlife and restaurant scene. Old Town, once dubbed the Paris of the East, is filled with lavishglass hotels and business centers.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Visit the living history of Old City
          </li>
          <li>
           Take part in a day tour around the city
          </li>
          <li>
           Go shopping at theCentral Market
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          12. Montreal, Canada
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200730" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 66.56%">
            <img alt="montreal-skyline-from" bgcolor="#325a70" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200730" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/montreal-skyline-from-1024x682.jpg","width":3305,"height":2204}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/montreal-skyline-from-1024x682.jpg","width":1024,"height":682}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/montreal-skyline-from-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/montreal-skyline-from-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
          <br/>
          The Quebecois cosmopolitan center, Montreal is home to an alluring mix of cuisine, festivals and culture with its irresistible pastries, breathtaking heritage such as the Notre-Dame Basilica, and its winter wonderlands of nearby ski resorts and ice hotels. Despite its modest size, its packed and you dont want to miss out on it.
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="montreal-skyline-from" height="426" src="http://cdn-media-2.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/montreal-skyline-from-1024x682.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.basiliquenddm.org/en/" target="_blank">
            Basilique Notre-Dame de Montral
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Go crazy at gallery-slash-curiosity-shop
           <a href="http://monastiraki.blogspot.ca/" target="_blank">
            Monastiraki
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Give the seafood a little taste at Le Filet
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          13. Berlin, Germany
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200733" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 54.22%">
            <img alt="Berlin-Ville" bgcolor="#576871" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200733" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Berlin-Ville-1024x556.jpg","width":1260,"height":685}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Berlin-Ville-1024x556.jpg","width":1024,"height":556}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Berlin-Ville-380x206.jpg","width":380,"height":206}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Berlin-Ville-380x206.jpg","width":380,"height":206}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="Berlin-Ville" height="347" src="http://cdn-media-1.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/Berlin-Ville-1024x556.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          A sobering and edgy reminder of the postwar atmosphere, from its fashion to its architecture to its history. But Berlin is a combo of museums, galleries, operas, guerrilla clubs and snack shacks that go beyond its dark history, making it almost reminiscent of 1980s New York.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Pay the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g187323-d196239-Reviews-Memorial_of_the_Berlin_Wall-Berlin.html" target="_blank">
            Berlin Wall Memorial
           </a>
           a visit
          </li>
          <li>
           Take a bus to
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g187323-d190520-Reviews-Museum_Island-Berlin.html" target="_blank">
            Museum Island
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Play the brilliant
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g187323-d6728190-Reviews-TeamEscape_Berlin-Berlin.html" target="_blank">
            TeamEscape Berlin
           </a>
           with some friends
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          14. Lhasa, Tibet
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200734" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 75%">
            <img alt="Lhasa Tibet China 11" bgcolor="#787076" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200734" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Lhasa-Tibet-China-11-1024x768.jpg","width":1600,"height":1200}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Lhasa-Tibet-China-11-1024x768.jpg","width":1024,"height":768}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Lhasa-Tibet-China-11-380x285.jpg","width":380,"height":285}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Lhasa-Tibet-China-11-380x285.jpg","width":380,"height":285}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="Lhasa Tibet China 11" height="480" src="http://cdn-media-2.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/Lhasa-Tibet-China-11-1024x768.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          The heart and soul of Tibet, deep in the Himalayan mountains, Lhasa remains to be a city of ancient wonder despite the modern Chinese influence. Its streets are bustling with people from all around the world and the city has become a cultural hybrid.Being seen as the real Tibet, Lhasa deserves a week of exploration to fully capture the vibes it possesses.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Take a walk around
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g294223-d319162-Reviews-Potala_Palace-Lhasa_Tibet.html" target="_blank">
            Potala Palace
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit the famous
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g294223-d325691-Reviews-Jokhang_Temple-Lhasa_Tibet.html" target="_blank">
            Jokhang Temple
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Relax at
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g294223-d325693-Reviews-Norbulingka_Precious_Stone_Garden-Lhasa_Tibet.html" target="_blank">
            Norbulingka
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          15. Cape Town, South Africa
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200736" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 55.63%">
            <img alt="capetown_apartments" bgcolor="#53708f" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200736" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/capetown_apartments-1024x570.jpg","width":1500,"height":836}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/capetown_apartments-1024x570.jpg","width":1024,"height":570}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/capetown_apartments-380x211.jpg","width":380,"height":211}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/capetown_apartments-380x211.jpg","width":380,"height":211}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="capetown_apartments" height="356" src="http://cdn-media-1.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/capetown_apartments-1024x570.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          Known as the Mother City with all of Mother Natures beautiful wonders, the proudly multicultural community that coexists in harmony gives Cape Town an exotic and delicious touch. The Table Mountain National Park is the most important attraction and in essence defines the city as a whole, and the gorgeous metropolis is filled with chalets, parks, Afro-chic decor and restaurants for all tastes.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Take a look at the mountains from a slightly different view via the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g312659-d481266-Reviews-Table_Mountain_Aerial_Cableway-Cape_Town_Central_Western_Cape.html" target="_blank">
            Table Mountain Aerial Cableway
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Attend a show at
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g312659-d3475763-Reviews-The_African_Dance_Theatre-Cape_Town_Central_Western_Cape.html" target="_blank">
            The African Dance Theatre
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g312659-d311012-Reviews-Two_Oceans_Aquarium-Cape_Town_Central_Western_Cape.html" target="_blank">
            Two Oceans Aquarium
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          16. Siem Reap, Cambodia
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200737" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 61.25%">
            <img alt="dsc_8153" bgcolor="#7a7869" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200737" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/dsc_8153-1024x628.jpg","width":4696,"height":2884}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/dsc_8153-1024x628.jpg","width":1024,"height":628}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/dsc_8153-380x233.jpg","width":380,"height":233}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/dsc_8153-380x233.jpg","width":380,"height":233}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="dsc_8153" height="392" src="http://cdn-media-2.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/dsc_8153-1024x628.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          Being one of thelargest religious complexes in the world, Siem Reap has become one of the most popular destination for tourists worldwide. The home of the temples of Angkor, Cambodias eighth wonder of the world, has reinvented itself into becoming the epicenter of the new Cambodia. With its temples, history, shopping stalls, food vendors, and world-class spas, you might want to spend a little more than just a couple of days here.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g297390-d552507-Reviews-Bayon_Temple-Siem_Reap_Siem_Reap_Province.html" target="_blank">
            Bayon Temple
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           See the wonders of the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g297390-d1727839-Reviews-Angkor_Archaeological_Park-Siem_Reap_Siem_Reap_Province.html" target="_blank">
            Angkor Archaeological Park
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Check out the must-see
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g297390-d4177819-Reviews-Sombai_Infused_Rice_Spirit_Shop-Siem_Reap_Siem_Reap_Province.html" target="_blank">
            Sombai Infused Rice Spirit Shop
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          17. Skopje, Republic of Macedonia
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-full wp-image-200738" style="max-width: 1024px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 75%">
            <img alt="SKO1_1_Skopje08" bgcolor="#828383" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-full wp-image-200738" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/SKO1_1_Skopje08.jpg","width":1024,"height":768}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/SKO1_1_Skopje08.jpg","width":1024,"height":768}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/SKO1_1_Skopje08-380x285.jpg","width":380,"height":285}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/SKO1_1_Skopje08-380x285.jpg","width":380,"height":285}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="SKO1_1_Skopje08" height="768" src="http://cdn-media-2.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/SKO1_1_Skopje08.jpg" width="1024"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          One of Europes most riveting and multifaceted cities, with a very historic vibe derived from all that survives from Skopjes Ottoman and Byzantine-erafrom hand-carved ornaments to fortresses. This is accentuated with a very contemporary culture with its bars, clubs and galleries.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g295110-d3220826-Reviews-Holocaust_Memorial_Centre-Skopje_Skopje_Region.html" target="_blank">
            Holocaust Memorial Centre
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Cross
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g295110-d3783814-Reviews-The_Stone_Bridge-Skopje_Skopje_Region.html" target="_blank">
            The Stone Bridge
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g295110-d2216683-Reviews-Memorial_House_of_Mother_Teresa-Skopje_Skopje_Region.html" target="_blank">
            Memorial House of Mother Teresa
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          18. Istanbul, Turkey
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200739" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 56.09%">
            <img alt="2252" bgcolor="#797672" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200739" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/2252-1024x575.jpg","width":1366,"height":768}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/2252-1024x575.jpg","width":1024,"height":575}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/2252-380x213.jpg","width":380,"height":213}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/2252-380x213.jpg","width":380,"height":213}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="2252" height="359" src="http://cdn-media-2.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/2252-1024x575.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          Istanbul is one of the hottest tourist attractions around nowadays. With its mosques, bazaars, Turkish baths, restaurants, galleries and clubs, its been dubbedthe Worlds Hippest City. Theres plenty to keep you busy during the day, from sightseeing to getting the ultimate Turkish treatment at a spa, but at night theres this
          <em>
           joie de vivre
          </em>
          sensation throughout when the clubs and restaurants are buzzing with action.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g293974-d296037-Reviews-Suleymaniye_Mosque-Istanbul.html" target="_blank">
            Suleymaniye Mosque
           </a>
           and the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g293974-d294497-Reviews-Hagia_Sophia_Museum_Church_Ayasofya-Istanbul.html" target="_blank">
            Hagia Sophia Museum
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit the chilling
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g293974-d294555-Reviews-Basilica_Cistern-Istanbul.html" target="_blank">
            Basilica Cistern
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Take a relaxing visit to
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g293974-d3626134-Reviews-Kilic_Ali_Pasa_Hamami-Istanbul.html" target="_blank">
            Kilic Ali Pasa Hamami
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          19. Hanoi, Vietnam
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-full wp-image-200740" style="max-width: 1024px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 75%">
            <img alt="Hanoi the huc bridge" bgcolor="#61654e" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-full wp-image-200740" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Hanoi-the-huc-bridge.jpg","width":1024,"height":768}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Hanoi-the-huc-bridge.jpg","width":1024,"height":768}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Hanoi-the-huc-bridge-380x285.jpg","width":380,"height":285}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Hanoi-the-huc-bridge-380x285.jpg","width":380,"height":285}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="Hanoi the huc bridge" height="768" src="http://cdn-media-1.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/Hanoi-the-huc-bridge.jpg" width="1024"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          This exotic city blends medieval and modern as they co-exist in an urban center with Parisianchic and Asian pace. Having survived American bombs and Russian planners, Hanoi re-emerged after economic reforms and is now scattered with huge mansions, grand boulevards, lakes, and parks, not to mention the 600 temples and pagodas. The City of the Soaring Dragon awaits you.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Visit the real Hanoi:
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g293924-d317503-Reviews-Old_Quarter-Hanoi.html" target="_blank">
            Old Quater
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Pay the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g293924-d447354-Reviews-Vietnamese_Women_s_Museum-Hanoi.html" target="_blank">
            Vietnamese Womens Museum
           </a>
           a visit
          </li>
          <li>
           Try out the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g293924-d2720375-Reviews-VietClimb-Hanoi.html" target="_blank">
            VietClimb
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          20. Vilnius, Lithuania
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200741" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 69.69%">
            <img alt="OLYMPUS DIGITAL CAMERA" bgcolor="#798075" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200741" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Vilnius_river-1024x714.jpg","width":3067,"height":2140}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Vilnius_river-1024x714.jpg","width":1024,"height":714}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Vilnius_river-380x265.jpg","width":380,"height":265}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Vilnius_river-380x265.jpg","width":380,"height":265}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="OLYMPUS DIGITAL CAMERA" height="446" src="http://cdn-media-1.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/Vilnius_river-1024x714.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          Curiously charming, eccentric and soulful. Lined with decadent and fragile Orthodox and Catholic churches, theres more to this capital than meets the eye as the underlying magic is what creates its soul. The true essence of boho spirit lurks around the reminders of loss and pain that only make it more captivating.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>

            Wrong Room
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g274951-d291081-Reviews-Vilnius_Old_Town-Vilnius_Vilnius_County.html" target="_blank">
            Old Town
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Pay the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g274951-d290801-Reviews-Holocaust_Museum_The_Green_House-Vilnius_Vilnius_County.html" target="_blank">
            Holocaust Museum
           </a>
           a visit
          </li>

         <p>

         <noscript>
          <img alt="PBK_Landing_Leaderboard" height="359" src="http://cdn-media-1.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/PBK_Landing_Leaderboard-1024x575.jpg" width="640"/>

         <div class="inner withClose" id="overlayInnerDiv" style="color: #2c2c2c;">
          <p>
           Bangkok is split into 50 unique districts filled with golden palaces, porcelain inlaid spires, and floating markets and food stalls. The olddistricts still possess the grit that the city used to have, which makes them a must-see for any first-time visitors. Thai cuisine is one to marvel at too with its diverse sweet, spicy, sour and salty flavors.

         <h2>
          22. Barcelona, Spain
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200743" style="max-width: 640px">

          Barcelona is Spains most cosmopolitan city, with its avant-garde chefs and its flamboyant street performers. Once home to Picasso, Barcelona has been revolutionary when it comes to art and despite the seeming aura of hedonism, its people are very dynamic and hardworking. The capital of Catalonia could keep you occupied for weeks so make sure you pay it a good visit.

          This is gondola central, with its canals, restaurants, romantic ambiance, Grand Canal palaces and marble churches. Venetians ignore the

            aqua alta
           </em>

         <p>
          Home to the tallest building in the world, the only seven-star hotel and the largest artificial islands, Dubai is the multifaceted cosmopolitan center of the future. Constantly full of surprises, Dubai is ever changing with its multiplying shopping malls, extraordinary architecture and delicious gourmet restaurants featuring a taste of places from all around the globe. In addition, you have the desert to explore: just rent a dune buggy and go crazy.

          Sun-kissed, sultry and shimmering. By day, its a must to hit the beach, walk about Miamis colorful Art Deco architecture, or dare to hit the envious South Beach celebrity scene. West of the city is the Everglades, the mosteccentric ecosystem in North America while to the North youve got the infamous Fort Lauderdale with its yachtsandmartinis. Miami is sweaty but glamorous and the party is always on, you take your pick!

         <p>
          History with an urban flair, thats Amsterdam. The gentle canals are a beautiful backdrop for the Jordaan and Rembrandtplein Square, and no one should miss out on the most moving experience of the Anne Frank House. Amsterdam is cosy and surrounded with artistictreasureslike the Van Gogh Museum. Although many tourists are only there to see the Red Light District, be sure to explore the rich history in all the houses that date back to the Golden Age.

         <h2>
          29. Varna, Bulgaria
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200752" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 66.56%">
            <img alt="image354-2" bgcolor="#64888c" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200752" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/image354-2-1024x682.jpg","width":1600,"height":1067}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/image354-2-1024x682.jpg","width":1024,"height":682}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/image354-2-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/image354-2-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="image354-2" height="426" src="http://cdn-media-1.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/image354-2-1024x682.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          This maritime capital is by far the most interesting and cosmopolitan town on the Black Sea coast as it is a combination of port city, naval base and seaside resort. How could it get any moreinteresting? Beautiful enormous parks, historic feel, Roman baths, museums and a buzzing restaurant scene, thats how!
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g295392-d1095828-Reviews-Varna_Archaeological_Museum-Varna_Varna_Province.html" target="_blank">
            Varna Archaeological Museum
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Watch history reveal itself at the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g295392-d555280-Reviews-Cathedral_of_the_Assumption_of_the_Virgin-Varna_Varna_Province.html" target="_blank">
            Cathedral of the Assumption of the Virgin
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Have some family fun at the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g295392-d4702484-Reviews-Amusement_Park_Varna-Varna_Varna_Province.html" target="_blank">
            Varna Amusement Park
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          30. Bali, Indonesia
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200753" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 63.44%">
            <img alt="390_16" bgcolor="#5c7c8f" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200753" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/390_16-1024x651.jpg","width":4304,"height":2737}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/390_16-1024x651.jpg","width":1024,"height":651}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/390_16-380x241.jpg","width":380,"height":241}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/390_16-380x241.jpg","width":380,"height":241}'/>

         <p>
          The saying that the best things come in small packages is very true when it comes to Bali because it is more than just small, its an Indonesian paradise. Listening to your bodys needs and pleasuring it with a massage on the beach or a sybaritic spa is first on your travel checklist. Then comes the shopping, the cuisine and the beautiful, lively nightlife, you will never get enough of the frangipani trees or the enchanting temple ceremonies.

          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>

           </a>
           a visit
          </li>

           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g469404-d2186624-Reviews-Chef_Dean_Cooking_Class-Seminyak_Bali.html" target="_blank">
            Chef Deans Cooking Class
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Go on a day tour with
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g297694-d1554699-Reviews-Bali_Adventure_Tours_Day_Tours-Denpasar_Bali.html" target="_blank">
            Bali Adventure Tours

           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 66.56%">
            <img alt="2014-05-16-Bucharest3" bgcolor="#818a7d" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200755" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/2014-05-16-Bucharest3-1024x682.jpg","width":3076,"height":2050}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/2014-05-16-Bucharest3-1024x682.jpg","width":1024,"height":682}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/2014-05-16-Bucharest3-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/2014-05-16-Bucharest3-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}'/>

          Most dont speak too fondly of this capital, but its perplexing. Thats its point! Its medieval and home to many of Romanias most historic churches. This is the place to leave your comfort zone and just go exploring all the elegant vibes of the 20th century, French-influenced architecture. Stick around for more than a day, and itll just make sense
          <em>
           .

         <h2>
          33. Lima, Peru
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-full wp-image-200756" style="max-width: 1024px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 75%">
            <img alt="Lima__Peru_by_Ghostofachild" bgcolor="#5c595b" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-full wp-image-200756" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Lima__Peru_by_Ghostofachild.jpg","width":1024,"height":768}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Lima__Peru_by_Ghostofachild.jpg","width":1024,"height":768}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Lima__Peru_by_Ghostofachild-380x285.jpg","width":380,"height":285}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Lima__Peru_by_Ghostofachild-380x285.jpg","width":380,"height":285}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="Lima__Peru_by_Ghostofachild" height="768" src="http://cdn-media-1.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/Lima__Peru_by_Ghostofachild.jpg" width="1024"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          Lima is for those willing to delve deep into a city to truly understand and unravel the beauty underneath the foggy and chaotic atmosphere. Limas beauties are humble, hiding amid the high rises where the pre-Columbian temples and colonial mansions lie. Lima also makes up for the aesthetics with a multitude of experiences, from museums filled with poetry to golf clubs and crowded nightclubs. This is what youd call a hot mess, dont miss it.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Have a gorgeously Peruvian meal at
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g294316-d2358313-Reviews-The_Lima_Gourmet_Company-Lima_Lima_Region.html" target="_blank">
            The Lima Gourmet Company
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Go shopping at the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g294316-d596436-Reviews-Shopping_Center_Larcomar_Centro_Comercial_Larcomar-Lima_Lima_Region.html" target="_blank">
            Centro Comercial Larcomar
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit thespending
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g294316-d1422223-Reviews-Magic_Water_Circuit-Lima_Lima_Region.html" target="_blank">
            Magic Water Circuit
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>

         <h2>
          36. Kyoto, Japan
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200759" style="max-width: 640px">

         <h2>
          37. Siena, Italy
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200760" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 66.56%">
            <img alt="siena" bgcolor="#5f5841" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200760" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/siena-1024x682.jpg","width":1800,"height":1200}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/siena-1024x682.jpg","width":1024,"height":682}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/siena-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/siena-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}'/>

         <p>
          This Tuscan town will take you back in time with its marvelous marble floors, artwork and heritage from the Middle Ages.The citys artistic glories are largely Gothic and that is transcendant in its cathedrals and the medieval tradition that involves bareback riders (dangerously) racing on cobblestones. Its thrilling: a must-see for any avid traveler.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Visit the

            Biblioteca Piccolomini
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           See the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g187902-d207831-Reviews-Siena_Cathedral-Siena_Tuscany.html" target="_blank">
            Siena Cathedral
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g187902-d195555-Reviews-Piazza_del_Campo-Siena_Tuscany.html" target="_blank">
            Piazza del Campo
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          38. Dublin, Ireland
         </h2>
         <p>

So with a little touch of salsa beats and adventurous activities from hiking through the rain forests or taking a train along the jungle, youve got yourself the ultimate Panamanian experience.

         <p>
          San Jos is often seen as a collection of outdated commercial buildings, but beyond this extremely superficial and uninformed analysis this is is a cosmopolitan city filled with department stores of all sorts, chic cafs, and fast-food restaurants making it the nations cultural hub.
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g309293-d299079-Reviews-National_Theater-San_Jose_San_Jose_Metro_Province_of_San_Jose.html" target="_blank">

           </a>

          <li>

           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g309293-d304311-Reviews-Precolumbian_Gold_Museum-San_Jose_San_Jose_Metro_Province_of_San_Jose.html" target="_blank">
            Precolumbian Gold Museum
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Get brave and go bungee jumping with
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g309293-d2173385-Reviews-Tropical_Bungee-San_Jose_San_Jose_Metro_Province_of_San_Jose.html" target="_blank">

         <h2>

         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200772" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 65.47%">
            <img alt="Castle-Ljubljana-Panorama" bgcolor="#6294a6" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200772" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Castle-Ljubljana-Panorama-1024x671.jpg","width":2008,"height":1317}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Castle-Ljubljana-Panorama-1024x671.jpg","width":1024,"height":671}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Castle-Ljubljana-Panorama-380x249.jpg","width":380,"height":249}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Castle-Ljubljana-Panorama-380x249.jpg","width":380,"height":249}'/>

         <noscript>
          <img alt="Castle-Ljubljana-Panorama" height="419" src="http://cdn-media-2.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/Castle-Ljubljana-Panorama-1024x671.jpg" width="640"/>

         <p>
          Ljubljana is a delicious cocktail of German, Mediterranean and Slovene influence seasoned with the old towns Baroque, Art Nouveau and Renaissance buildings. The biggest perk has got to be everything is such a short distance away, just go for a walk or take a bike! The beloved city is also a student community, which means the alt-lifestyle gives it a different vibe.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>

           </a>
           is a must!
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit theatmospheric main plaza;
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g274873-d298648-Reviews-Preseren_Square-Ljubljana_Upper_Carniola_Region.html" target="_blank">
            Preseren Square
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Dont miss out on the urban cultural centre of
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g274873-d734854-Reviews-Metelkova-Ljubljana_Upper_Carniola_Region.html" target="_blank">
            Metelkova
           </a>

         <h2>
          49. Copenhagen, Denmark
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200764" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 66.88%">
            <img alt="copenhagen-canal-shops1" bgcolor="#665f5f" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200764" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/copenhagen-canal-shops1-1024x685.jpg","width":1222,"height":818}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/copenhagen-canal-shops1-1024x685.jpg","width":1024,"height":685}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/copenhagen-canal-shops1-380x254.jpg","width":380,"height":254}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/copenhagen-canal-shops1-380x254.jpg","width":380,"height":254}'/>

         </noscript>
         <p>
          What was once a Viking fishing settlement has transformed into the coolest, most cosmopolitan and most exciting city in Scandinavia, while holding on tothe traces of Norse explorers that keep its culture and history truly rich. Like all the best places, it has a blend of modern and historic, making it not just a great tourist destination but also one of the worlds most livable cities.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>

           </a>

            Nyhavn
           </a>
           a visit!
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g189541-d207266-Reviews-Nationalmuseet-Copenhagen_Zealand.html" target="_blank">

It embraces its historic legacies, fine art and absolutely delicious food. Rome is intriguing and will have you experiencing excitement with all your senses.

         <h2>
          <span style="color: #333333;">
           51. Singapore, Singapore
          </span>
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200782" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 62.5%">
            <img alt="singapore" bgcolor="#73797c" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200782" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/singapore-1024x641.jpg","width":1399,"height":876}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/singapore-1024x641.jpg","width":1024,"height":641}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/singapore-380x237.jpg","width":380,"height":237}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/singapore-380x237.jpg","width":380,"height":237}'/>

          </span>

         </noscript>
         <p>
          One of the most enjoyable, seemingly science fiction comic inspired cities in Southeast Asia from beginning to end. You begin at one of the worlds best airports and take a zippy MRT train line without a single care given for the traffic. Whether youre up for astroll through fashion emporiums andantique shops, or youre more interested in the city parks or the citys clubs, Singapore has got it all. The city is colorful, soulful and has a thriving creative environment!
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Dont miss out on

            The Escape Hunt Experience
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g294265-d310900-Reviews-Singapore_Botanic_Gardens-Singapore.html" target="_blank">
            Singapore Botanic Gardens
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Try out the super awesome
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g294265-d1382651-Reviews-Flight_Experience_Flight_Simulator-Singapore.html" target="_blank">
            Flight Simulator
           </a>

          Indulge in fresh pastries, window shopping, espressos and the warmly lit 1930s-era cafs, or take a walk along the seaside. At Bairro Alto youve got many restaurants with jazz and reggae vibes filling the air and nightclubs scattered all over the town. Lisbons Gothic cathedrals, monasteries and museums all accentuate this lovely city.

          Within the atmospheric walls where Split came to life, youve got a balance of tradition and modernity with many many bars, restaurants and shops. Its coastal mountains are the perfect backdrop to the Adriatic, where you can chill and appreciate the cityscape. While people used to cross Split to get where they wanted to go, the city has renovated itself to become exactly where people want to be.
         </p>

          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>

          </li>

         <h2>

          Vibrant, old-school and filled with precious architecture. After Hurricane Katrina broke the levee, New Orleans has managed to rebuild itself with echoing sweet jazz and blues beats, spontaneous dancing and mouthwatering aromas from unexpected corners. Its a great city for late afternoon walks, meant for the ones willing to admire its subtle charm.

           Things to do:

           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g60864-d108045-Reviews-New_Orleans_City_Park-New_Orleans_Louisiana.html" target="_blank">

           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>

            <img alt="0ae556d3-d8a2-403a-9da5-9932d6ffa875" bgcolor="#b2b3a9" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200776" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/0ae556d3-d8a2-403a-9da5-9932d6ffa875-1024x703.png","width":1177,"height":809}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/0ae556d3-d8a2-403a-9da5-9932d6ffa875-1024x703.png","width":1024,"height":703}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/0ae556d3-d8a2-403a-9da5-9932d6ffa875-380x261.png","width":380,"height":261}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/0ae556d3-d8a2-403a-9da5-9932d6ffa875-380x261.png","width":380,"height":261}'/>

          This constantly pulsating and hypnotizing metropolis will surprise you with the chaos at your arrival, but soon youll get drawn way too deep. As long as youre not looking for solitude, the City of the Thousand Minarets is the perfect place to explore and experience Egyptian history and culture.

           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          <span style="color: #333333;">
