          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-full wp-image-200785" style="max-width: 1024px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 66.31%">
            <img alt="Sydney-Australia-8" bgcolor="#515070" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-full wp-image-200785" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Sydney-Australia-8.jpg","width":1024,"height":679}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Sydney-Australia-8.jpg","width":1024,"height":679}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Sydney-Australia-8-380x251.jpg","width":380,"height":251}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/Sydney-Australia-8-380x251.jpg","width":380,"height":251}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="Sydney-Australia-8" height="679" src="http://cdn-media-2.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/Sydney-Australia-8.jpg" width="1024"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          Sydney is attractive at any time of day, so keep your eyes wide open! Its famous for its National Parks and its super eventful evenings of undercover bar hunting, sporting events to support, underground bands to check out or a super crazy party to crash. The citys glamorous but oh-so-casual at the same time making it such a relaxed but vibrant environment. Everybody loves to tan at the beautiful golden beaches, enjoy the exciting food scene and explore the very subtle touches of history.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Go to the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g255060-d257842-Reviews-Sydney_Harbour-Sydney_New_South_Wales.html" target="_blank">
            Sydney Harbour
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Take a
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g255060-d2534313-Reviews-Bondi_to_Coogee_Beach_Coastal_Walk-Sydney_New_South_Wales.html" target="_blank">
            beach walk from Bondi to Coogee
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g255060-d257278-Reviews-Sydney_Opera_House-Sydney_New_South_Wales.html" target="_blank">
            Sydney Opera House
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          <span style="color: #333333;">
           57. Seoul,South Korea
          </span>
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200777" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 66.56%">
            <img alt="53aca62e0ef3a3c6347f74fc" bgcolor="#707d9a" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200777" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/53aca62e0ef3a3c6347f74fc-1024x683.jpg","width":1507,"height":1006}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/53aca62e0ef3a3c6347f74fc-1024x683.jpg","width":1024,"height":683}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/53aca62e0ef3a3c6347f74fc-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/53aca62e0ef3a3c6347f74fc-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="53aca62e0ef3a3c6347f74fc" height="426" src="http://cdn-media-2.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/53aca62e0ef3a3c6347f74fc-1024x683.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          Seoul is a very interesting mix of everything from night markets to the infamous K-Pop, but of course it goes beyond what we all vaguely know about it. The city is filled with temples, skyscrapers and majestic palaces everywhere in addition to the 21st century urban edge in design and culture. Ten and a half million people reside in this metropolis and it almost never goes to sleep because the day is for a lovely morning visit to a temple followed by a visit to a teahouse, and the night is for the night markets and the Hongdae or Itaewon party life!
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Visit
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g294197-d554537-Reviews-The_War_Memorial_of_Korea-Seoul.html" target="_blank">
            The War Memorial of Korea
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Go for a hike at the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g294197-d554528-Reviews-Bukhansan_National_Park-Seoul.html" target="_blank">
            Bukhansan National Park
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Pay the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g294197-d1862210-Reviews-Seoul_Arts_Center-Seoul.html" target="_blank">
            Seoul Arts Centre
           </a>
           a visit
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          <span style="color: #333333;">
           58. Milan, Italy
          </span>
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200780" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 68.75%">
            <img alt="milan-city-world-444313" bgcolor="#6a8e97" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200780" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/milan-city-world-444313-1024x704.jpg","width":1600,"height":1101}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/milan-city-world-444313-1024x704.jpg","width":1024,"height":704}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/milan-city-world-444313-380x261.jpg","width":380,"height":261}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/milan-city-world-444313-380x261.jpg","width":380,"height":261}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="milan-city-world-444313" height="440" src="http://cdn-media-1.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/milan-city-world-444313-1024x704.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          The worlds top fashion capital means glamor, grace and Gucci. Milan is a well-dressed and chic engine room for the countrys economy. Filled with true treasures like da Vincis The Last Supper showing just how much Milans creative streak has an impact. Everyone has been here on the runways from Prada to Versace to Dolce &amp; Gabbana, so why not get dressed up and come along?
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g187849-d195239-Reviews-Milan_Cathedral_Duomo-Milan_Lombardy.html" target="_blank">
            Milan Cathedral
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Pay the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g187849-d4501654-Reviews-Dialogo_nel_Buio-Milan_Lombardy.html" target="_blank">
            Dialogo nel Buio
           </a>
           a visit
          </li>
          <li>
           Go crazy with the credit card at
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g187849-d1907083-Reviews-La_Rinascente-Milan_Lombardy.html" target="_blank">
            La Rinascente
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          59. Chicago, USA
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200778" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 56.09%">
            <img alt="chicago_street" bgcolor="#6d7173" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200778" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/chicago_street-1024x575.jpg","width":1202,"height":676}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/chicago_street-1024x575.jpg","width":1024,"height":575}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/chicago_street-380x213.jpg","width":380,"height":213}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/chicago_street-380x213.jpg","width":380,"height":213}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="chicago_street" height="359" src="http://cdn-media-2.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/chicago_street-1024x575.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          The Windy City will blow you away, trust me. Theres always something going on here, from high-flying architecture to peanut butter and banana topped waffles for breakfast, could thingsget any better? Chicago is great festivals and Lollapalooza is a must-see because when everybodys head banging to the beat, you really dont want to miss out on the fun. Art museums come in all genres: impressionist, psychedelic or outsider? Take your pick! Chicago will surely keep you busy and entertained.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Attend the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g35805-d2412346-Reviews-Million_Dollar_Quartet-Chicago_Illinois.html" target="_blank">
            Million Dollar Quartet
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g35805-d278811-Reviews-Millennium_Park-Chicago_Illinois.html" target="_blank">
            Millennium Park
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           Have a laugh at
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g35805-d266629-Reviews-Second_City-Chicago_Illinois.html" target="_blank">
            Second City
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          60. Prague, Czech Republic
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span class="lazy-div aligncenter size-large wp-image-200781" style="max-width: 640px">
           <span class="lazy-div-placeholder" style="padding-bottom: 66.56%">
            <img alt="prague-x2" bgcolor="#607daa" class="lazy-img aligncenter size-large wp-image-200781" data-bttrlazyloading-lg='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-2.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/prague-x2-1024x683.jpg","width":1280,"height":854}' data-bttrlazyloading-md='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/prague-x2-1024x683.jpg","width":1024,"height":683}' data-bttrlazyloading-sm='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/prague-x2-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}' data-bttrlazyloading-xs='{"src":"http:\/\/cdn-media-1.lifehack.org\/wp-content\/files\/2014\/09\/prague-x2-380x253.jpg","width":380,"height":253}'/>
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <noscript>
          <img alt="prague-x2" height="426" src="http://cdn-media-2.lifehack.org/wp-content/files/2014/09/prague-x2-1024x683.jpg" width="640"/>
         </noscript>
         <p>
          Super bohemian and fairytale-like for the travelers who want to immerse themselves wholly into another culture. Prague is a European hotspot with art galleries ranging from Gothic pieces to collections of 20th-century surrealists, constructivists and cubists. The city is also quite famous for making some of the worlds best brews so grab a pint and head on an urban exploration of the alluring and rather quirky Prague.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Things to do:
          </strong>
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Always visit the originals;
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g274707-d275451-Reviews-Old_Town_Stare_Mesto-Prague_Bohemia.html" target="_blank">
            Old Town
           </a>
           or Stare Mesto
          </li>
          <li>
           Try out the
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g274707-d1576262-Reviews-Prague_On_Segway-Prague_Bohemia.html" target="_blank">
            Prague on Segway
           </a>
           experience
          </li>
          <li>
           Visit the spectacular
           <a href="http://www.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g274707-d318606-Reviews-National_Theater_Narodni_divadlo-Prague_Bohemia.html" target="_blank">
            National Theatre
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <p class="call-action">
          Love this article?
          <a class="facebook-share-popup-link" data-link="http://www.lifehack.org/articles/lifestyle/the-ultimate-wanderlist-60-cities-visit-before-you-die.html" href="#">
           Share it with your friends on Facebook
          </a>
         </p>
